It is the holiest city for Hindus. It is the Avimukta Kshetra where Purusha and Prakriti dwelt first. Varanasi is Shiva KShetra. It was a Vishnu KShetra before. \r\n Varanasi is settle next to the left banks of the Ganga and numerous Ghats line up their. Varanasi is also the dwelling place of Shiva where he lives as the Vishweshwar Linga in the Kashi Viswanath Mandir at Gyanvapi.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe Assi River\nThe Assi River flows into the Ganga at the famous Assi Ghat. The Assi Ghat is famous as the dwelling place of Goswami Tulsidas ji.\r\n The Ramacharita Manas was composed here. The Assi Ghat is famous for the early morning Kirtans and cultural activities. The Ganga Aarti takes place here.\r\n The Assi River flows next to the Baba Kinarama Asthal. The river has unfortunately been polluted beyond recognition by sewers emptying into it.\r\n Efforts are being made to revive it.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\nPlaces in Varanasi\n\n\n\n\nBheem Chandi\nBheem Chandi,Rameshwar\n\n\n\n\n\nRameshwar Mahadev Mandir on the Varuna\nThird stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nLast stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama Yatra\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBhairav Nath Mandir.\nOn the Rajatalab to Jansa Road\n\n\n\n\n\nPancha Pandava Mandir, Varanasi\n fourth stop on the Kashi Panchkoshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nFifth and last stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nMap of Varanasi\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCONTACT\n\n\nContact us for any query about Varanasi and we'll get back to you within 24 hours.\n Varanasi, India\n +91 9335874326\n varanasikshetra@gmail.com\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSend\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n©Champak's World\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN

It is the holiest city for Hindus. It is the Avimukta Kshetra where Purusha and Prakriti dwelt first. Varanasi is Shiva KShetra. It was a Vishnu KShetra before. \r\n Varanasi is settle next to the left banks of the Ganga and numerous Ghats line up their. Varanasi is also the dwelling place of Shiva where he lives as the Vishweshwar Linga in the Kashi Viswanath Mandir at Gyanvapi.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe Assi River\nThe Assi River flows into the Ganga at the famous Assi Ghat. The Assi Ghat is famous as the dwelling place of Goswami Tulsidas ji.\r\n The Ramacharita Manas was composed here. The Assi Ghat is famous for the early morning Kirtans and cultural activities. The Ganga Aarti takes place here.\r\n The Assi River flows next to the Baba Kinarama Asthal. The river has unfortunately been polluted beyond recognition by sewers emptying into it.\r\n Efforts are being made to revive it.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\nPlaces in Varanasi\n\n\n\n\nBheem Chandi\nBheem Chandi,Rameshwar\n\n\n\n\n\nRameshwar Mahadev Mandir on the Varuna\nThird stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nLast stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama Yatra\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBhairav Nath Mandir.\nOn the Rajatalab to Jansa Road\n\n\n\n\n\nPancha Pandava Mandir, Varanasi\n fourth stop on the Kashi Panchkoshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nKapil Dhara, Varanasi\nFifth and last stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nMap of Varanasi\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCONTACT\n\n\nContact us for any query about Varanasi and we'll get back to you within 24 hours.\n Varanasi, India\n +91 9335874326\n varanasikshetra@gmail.com\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSend\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n©Champak's World\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN

It is the holiest city for Hindus. It is the Avimukta Kshetra where Purusha and Prakriti dwelt first. Varanasi is Shiva KShetra. It was a Vishnu KShetra before. \r\n Varanasi is settle next to the left banks of the Ganga and numerous Ghats line up their. Varanasi is also the dwelling place of Shiva where he lives as the Vishweshwar Linga in the Kashi Viswanath Mandir at Gyanvapi.\r\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThe Assi River\nThe Assi River flows into the Ganga at the famous Assi Ghat. The oldest surviving Mandir in Varanasi. The Shikhara of this Mandir is the only one that survived the Islamic and British Invasions.\r\nKardameshwar Mahadev is a must visit.\r\n\r\n \nCreation of Rishi Kardam and the other Prajapatis.\n\r\n Rishi Kardam is one of the Prajapatis created by Brahma Ji. Bhrigu, Marichi,\r\nAtri, Daksha, Kardam, Pulastya, Pulaha, Angira and Kratu are some of the Prajapatis.\r\n\r\nRishi Kardam and Dharma were created from the shadow of Bhagwan Brahma.\r\n\r\nBrahma created Rishi Marichi from his eyes, Rishi Bhrigu came from his heart.\r\nRishi Angira came from his head,Rishi Pulaha from his Vyan Vayu and Rishi Pulatsya from his Udana Vaya.\r\n\r\nRishi Vashishtha the Rajguru of Ayodhya came from his Samana Vayu. Rishi Kratu from his Apan Vayu.\r\nAtri Rishi descended from the ear of Brahma.\r\nNarada came from the lap of Brahma. Another Prajapati was Daksha.\r\n\n\nMarriage and children of Rishi Kardam\n\r\n Brahma Ji ordered Rishi Kardam to tapasya and accordingly the Rishi undertook Tapasya.\r\n After this Rishi Kardam was married to Devahuti the daughter of Manu and Shatrupa. Rishi Kardam and Devahuti were the first couple to undertake creation in the earthly way.\r\n The Rishi couple had nine daughters.These were Kala, Anusuya, Shraddha, Havirbhu, Gati, Shanti, Krita,Khyati and Arundhati.\r\n\r\n The daughters were married off. Rishi Kardam took sanyas leaving aside the grihastha ashram.\r\n \nRevised on 09-Sep-2019 by Champak Roy\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir, Mata Mandir\nMata Mandir\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir,Mata Mandir detail.\nMurti detail\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir Rudrashtakam, Varanasi\nKardameshwar Mandir. first stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir Sarovar, Varanasi\nKardameshwar Mandir Sarovar\n\n\n\n\n\nTo see more images please click here\n\n\n\n\nMap of Shri Kardameshwar Mahadev Mandir area, Varanasi\n\n\n\n\n\n\n NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN

The Shikhara of this Mandir is the only one that survived the Islamic and British Invasions.\r\nKardameshwar Mahadev is a must visit.\r\n\r\n \nCreation of Rishi Kardam and the other Prajapatis.\n\r\n Rishi Kardam is one of the Prajapatis created by Brahma Ji. Bhrigu, Marichi,\r\nAtri, Daksha, Kardam, Pulastya, Pulaha, Angira and Kratu are some of the Prajapatis.\r\n\r\nRishi Kardam and Dharma were created from the shadow of Bhagwan Brahma.\r\n\r\nBrahma created Rishi Marichi from his eyes, Rishi Bhrigu came from his heart.\r\nRishi Angira came from his head,Rishi Pulaha from his Vyan Vayu and Rishi Pulatsya from his Udana Vaya.\r\n\r\nRishi Vashishtha the Rajguru of Ayodhya came from his Samana Vayu. Rishi Kratu from his Apan Vayu.\r\nAtri Rishi descended from the ear of Brahma.\r\nNarada came from the lap of Brahma. Another Prajapati was Daksha.\r\n\n\nMarriage and children of Rishi Kardam\n\r\n Brahma Ji ordered Rishi Kardam to tapasya and accordingly the Rishi undertook Tapasya.\r\n After this Rishi Kardam was married to Devahuti the daughter of Manu and Shatrupa. Rishi Kardam and Devahuti were the first couple to undertake creation in the earthly way.\r\n The Rishi couple had nine daughters.These were Kala, Anusuya, Shraddha, Havirbhu, Gati, Shanti, Krita,Khyati and Arundhati.\r\n\r\n The daughters were married off. Rishi Kardam took sanyas leaving aside the grihastha ashram.\r\n \nRevised on 09-Sep-2019 by Champak Roy\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir, Mata Mandir\nMata Mandir\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir,Mata Mandir detail.\nMurti detail\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir Rudrashtakam, Varanasi\nKardameshwar Mandir. first stop on the Panchkoshi parikrama.\n\n\n\n\n\nKardameshwar Mandir Sarovar, Varanasi\nKardameshwar Mandir Sarovar\n\n\n\n\n\nTo see more images please click here\n\n\n\n\nMap of Shri Kardameshwar Mahadev Mandir area, Varanasi\n\n\n\n\n\n NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN NaN
